Amazwi Omlobi 
Lendaba ibunjwe yalolongelwa phezu kwengqikithi yezehlakalo ezake zenzeka. Ngalesisizathu-ke ngibone kuranele ukuba ngihlalukise ukuthi amagama abalingiswa abakuyona ngamagama njc engizisungulcle wana emqondweni wami, akukho gama elithathelwe kumuntu odla noma kumbe owake wadla anhlamvana. Uma kuthuke kwenzeka igama lomlingiswa othize okulendaba larana ncimishi nelomuntu okhona noma awake wabakhona phansi komthunzi welanga, lokho kuyobe kwenzeke ngcngxaphephc nje ebcngingayisophilc. Futhi-ke akukho muntu ebenginenhloso yokumhlambalaza ngokuloba ngaye utho olulumclayo kulendaba. 
  Ngiyethula kinina nonke muzi wakwethu, ngethemba lokuthi lencwadi iyokuba njengetshe esivivaneni sempilo.

UNTOMBI UYAHLABEKA 
KwakungoLwcsine uma ngifika ckhaya ngamaholidc ascbusika, ingani uNtombi wayesesheshe wahamba ukuphindcla ekhaya, esuka kimi csikoleni cngasc ngifundisa kuso sascM tholankanyiso. Ngifika ckhaya nje ngifiea elelc ebubula yikugula.

Iminyaka lena yedlula njengonyazi. Nampa nabantwana sebezisebenzela, sesidla izinyoni zabo. Khona manjenje sesizokuzwa sebethi bathanda ukuzakhela eyabo imizi. Nakulokho-ke asiyikusola lutho, ngoba umlibo wakwaGombela uzobe usuwanda.' 
  Ngathula ngathula ngiyilokhu ngicabanga ukusuka kwezinto phansi, ukubonana kwami noNtombi, ukuhlupheka kwami ngokugula kukaNtombi, ukubonana kwami noLizzie, nokunethezeka kwami lapho sengimthathile esengumkami.

t I I ~ 
K wathi lapho sengikuphimisela lokho engangikucahanga, ngathi, 'Lizzie, ngimelwe ukuba ngikhombise ukubonga kwami mntanomunlu, ngoba wangibulha ngisezibini, futhi ngihluphekile, ngiyimpof'lIla engenalutho. Wena awuzange ubeke izizathu eziningi zokusola ukuthi umfelwa ungamthanda kanjani umgane nokwenza enabantwana, kanti wena uyintombi. Konke lokho wakushaya indiva, waqoka lokho okuqokayo. Namhlanje sesiqede amashumi amabili nesihlanu eminyaka siyilokhu sibambisene kulelijoka esazikhethela lona. Namhlanje abantwana sebeyazibonela nabo abakwenzayo empilweni yalomhlaba. Konke lokho kungen'xa yakho nothando lwakho, kungenxa yemikhuleko yakho obucela ngayo eNkosini ukuba ungisize ukufeza isifiso sikanina walababantwana kanye nesicelo asicela kuwe ephusheni, sokuthi uzakubabheka yini lababantwana. Ubabhekile-ke Moatludi, nokwenza uyintombi yomTswana. Awukhethanga bala lamuntu kumbe ubuzwe, kodwa wakhetha lokho uthando lwakho olwakuholela kukho. Nakhu namhla~e sifezekile isicelo sikaNtombi asenza kimi elele ecansini lokufa, ukuthi ngizobheka abantwana futhi ngikholwe na?' 
  Ngambona uLizzie esegobodisile ebheke phansi, kanti naye uphezu kwemicabango ejulile. Ngamuzwa esethi, 'Konke kwenzeka ngamandla kaNkulunkulu, kuphela thina esifanele ukukwenza ukubonga uMdali ngakho konke asenzele khona.' Naye wawasho lawo, wathula walhi zumbu. Kwathi ngesikade wathi, 'Awusahlabi James, sibonge iminyaka engaka sishadile!' 
  Vebo, kwakufanele sibonge, ngoba konke lokhu akwenzekanga ngokuhlakanipha kwethu, kodwa ngenxa yom usa kaNkulunkulu. 'Vebo, Lizzie, ngizoyolhenga imvu kwaKolimani, sihlabe sibonge uMdali ngakho konke asenzele khona empilweni yethu. Sekuyolhi noma sifa, sofa sesazi ukuthi abantwana sibaphile ifa_ elingapheliyo - imfundo noku- 
196 
kholwa. Impela, ngangingazi ukulhi namhlanje izinyembezi zami ziyobe sezesuliwe, ngangiyilokhu ngilhi mahlayana, mahlayana, zaze zesulwa izinyembezi.' 
  Sayihlaba imvu, senza umgidi omkhulu wokuzibongela iminyaka engamashumi amabili nesihlanu sishadile. NawoThokozani noThern bin kosi sabazisa masinyane ukuba beze ekhaya kuleyompelaviki esasizokuba nomgidi ngayo. UNobulembu yena wayenesa kuso isibhedlela lapho unina ashonela khona eTempe. Vena-ke wayehlala nathi ekhaya, kungenjengoThokozani owayeseWelkom noThembinkosi owayeseKroonstad. 
  Kwabamnandi kwadela ngalolusuku lomgidi. Kwakukhona nomakhelwane nezihlobo. Kwathi lapho sebehlakazekile bonke abantu, sasala thina abekhaya. Kwakuyimina kanye nomkami uLizzie noThokozani noThembinkosi noNobulembu. Sasesihlezi sonke etafuleni, sidla ukudla kwakusihlwa. Unina wabantwana uLizzie wayebalshela ukuthi umuntu ukuze abe ngumuntu emhlabeni kumelwe ukuba ethembele kuNkulunkulu, amthande ngayoyonke inhliziyo yakhe, nangawowonke umphefumulo wakhe, nomakhelwane wakhe njengalokhu ezithanda yena. 
  Lokhu uLizzie ayekutshela abantwana kwakuyiqiniso yena ayephila ngalo kuyoyonke impilo yomshado wethu. Waphendukela kubantwana wathi, 'Bantabami, mina noyihlo ngowamashumi amabili nanhlanu lonyaka siganene. Sinikhulisile, sanifundisa, sanenzela konke ebesifanele ukuba sinenzele khona njengabazali. Niyasebenza nonke ngothi lwenu. Vazini-ke ukuthi noma sesifa, asinalo igazi ezandleni zelhu. U rna sesingasekho, anibobhekana, nibhekane, futhi nenze konke ngokukholwa.' 
  Angihlaba lawomazwi kaLizzie, angikhumbllza amazwi kaNtombi awasho elele embhedeni wokllfa, 'Ubheke abantwana, IIkholwe, ukholwe.' Konke lokho sasikwenzile noLizzie. Sababheka abantwana, sakholwa, sakholwa!
